export interface ButtonCommons {
    block: boolean;
    circular: boolean;
    disabledFocusable: boolean;
    iconPosition: 'before' | 'after';
    outline: boolean;
    primary: boolean;
    size: 'small' | 'medium' | 'large';
    subtle: boolean;
    transparent: boolean;
}

    disabled?: boolean;
